TITLE       KeV neutron radiative capture and total cross         2037400100021 
            section of 50,52,53Cr, 54,57Fe and 62,64Ni            2037400100022 
FACILITY   (VDG,2GERKFK) Pulsed 3 MV Van de Graaff at Karlsruhe.  2037400100023 
INC-SOURCE (P-LI7)    Li-7(p,n)Be-7 reaction. Relatively thick    2037400100024 
            (150 keV) lithium target.  Proton pulse 1ns, 500kHz   2037400100025 
            repetition.                                           2037400100026 
METHOD     (TOF)    Time of flight. Path = 2 m.                   2037400100027 
SAMPLE     In the capture measurement, the sample to be analyzed  2037400100028 
           was interchanged with a carbon sample and a gold sample2037400100029 
           for background and neutron flux determination,         2037400100030 
           respectively. The sample material was pressed into     2037400100031 
           flat cylindrical bronze containers with a diameter of  2037400100032 
           8 cm. Because of the small amount of 64Ni available, a 2037400100033 
           bronze container of 4.5 cm diameter had to be used.    2037400100034 
           The gold sample was a disc of 9 cm dia. x 0.1 cm       2037400100035 
           thickness. The carbon samples were graphite discs      2037400100036 
           chosen to match the scattering cross section of the    2037400100037 
            analyzed sample.                                      2037400100038 
DETECTOR   (STANK)    Scintillator tank, approx. 800 liters       2037400100039 
PART-DET   (G)    Gammas.                                         2037400100040 
ANALYSIS   (AREA) Radiation widths (broad levels) and capture     2037400100041 
            areas (narrow levels) extracted with area analysis    2037400100042 
            code TACASI (Froehner, report GA-6906,1966), using    2037400100043 
            known neutron widths where available.                 2037400100044 
           (SHAPE) Neutron widths determined by multi-level       2037400100045 
            least-squares fit to transmission data, R-matrix      2037400100046 
            formalism. Inelastic channel taken into account for   2037400100047 
            Fe-57 above 14 keV.                                   2037400100048 
MONITOR    (79-AU-197(N,G)79-AU-198,,SIG)                         2037400100049 
            As reported by D.Kompe, Nucl.Phys.A133(1969)513.      2037400100050 
            see entry 20358.                                      2037400100051 
MONIT-REF  (20358035,D.Kompe,J,NP/A,133,513,1969)                 2037400100052 
CORRECTION .Cross section data were corrected for                 2037400100053 
              time-independent background,                        2037400100054 
              time-  dependent background(measured with C sample),2037400100055 
              sample admixtures (O in oxides, isotopic impurities)2037400100056 
              unrecorded pulse height spectrum fraction below     2037400100057 
                     3 MeV threshold,                             2037400100058 
              intrinsic tank efficiency (escape of entire cascade)2037400100059 
           .Radiation width extraction included corrections       2037400100060 
            for                                                   2037400100061 
              self-shielding,                                     2037400100062 
              multiple interactions (Monte Carlo treatment),      2037400100063 
              instrumental resolution,                            2037400100064 
              influence of nearby resonances.                     2037400100065 
ERR-ANALYS .Cross section errors include uncertainties from       2037400100066 
              counting statistics,                                2037400100067 
              background subtraction,                             2037400100068 
              spectrum fractions,                                 2037400100069 
              standard.                                           2037400100070 
           .Uncertainty in energy scale and resonance energies    2037400100071 
            estimated as 0.3%.                                    2037400100072 
           .Neutron and radiation width uncertainties calculated  2037400100073 
            from transmission and capture yield uncertainties     2037400100074 
            by error propagation through least-squares fit.       2037400100075 
COMMENT    .Capture cross section data are capture yields divided 2037400100076 
            by sample thickness in at./b, equal to true cross     2037400100077 
            section only where effects of sample thickness (self- 2037400100078 
            shielding, multiple collisions) and resolution are    2037400100079 
            negligible.                                           2037400100080
